If you set any of the colors on the body or a elements you must set all of them.
The colors used are:
color: rgb(0,0,0) from browser settings and background: rgb(255,255,255)
In HTML the color attributes are text, bgcolor, link, alink and vlink. In CSS the attributes are color and background-color. Some users have browser defaults set to white text on a black background, so setting one color without setting the others can result in black text on a black background.

1417 <div readonly="" class="sc-jcguBR eNfFTW sc-itScQp sc-eBLtXY jdNZjs haEues">

1418

If you set any of the colors on the body or a elements you must set all of them.
The colors used are:
color: rgb(0,0,0) from browser settings and background: rgb(255,255,255)
In HTML the color attributes are text, bgcolor, link, alink and vlink. In CSS the attributes are color and background-color. Some users have browser defaults set to white text on a black background, so setting one color without setting the others can result in black text on a black background.
Line 1418 WCAG 2.1 AA F24 Section 508 (2017) AA F24

1594

If you set any of the colors on the body or a elements you must set all of them.
The colors used are:
color: rgb(0,0,0) from browser settings and background: rgb(255,255,255)
In HTML the color attributes are text, bgcolor, link, alink and vlink. In CSS the attributes are color and background-color. Some users have browser defaults set to white text on a black background, so setting one color without setting the others can result in black text on a black background.
Line 1594 WCAG 2.1 AA F24 Section 508 (2017) AA F24

1781

If you set any of the colors on the body or a elements you must set all of them.
The colors used are:
color: rgb(0,0,0) from browser settings and background: rgb(255,255,255)
In HTML the color attributes are text, bgcolor, link, alink and vlink. In CSS the attributes are color and background-color. Some users have browser defaults set to white text on a black background, so setting one color without setting the others can result in black text on a black background.
Line 1781 WCAG 2.1 AA F24 Section 508 (2017) AA F24
